Naturally hazy. 4.1% ABV. Serve cold.

            <div class="beer-carousel-overlay__image">
             <img src="/-/media/mainsite/Beers/Past-Masters/1926-oatmeal-porter.png"/>
            </div>
            <div class="beer-carousel-overlay__info">
             <h3 class="heading heading--med heading--underline-narrow-thick-alt heading--overline-narrow-alt">
              Past Masters 1926
             </h3>
             <div class="beer-carousel-overlay__description">
              <p>
               This distinguished Porter pours a rich, dark colour, with the black malt making its presence felt in a deliciously dry bitterness. Notes of coffee and dark chocolate emerge amid fruitiness from the American hops, while Northumbrian oats contribute to a surprisingly smooth mouthfeel.
              </p>
             </div>
             <div class="beer-carousel-overlay__cyclops">
              <ul>
               <li class="sight">
                <svg class="icon">
                 <use id="beer-carousel-overlay__cyclops--sight-icon" xlink:href="#svg-eye">
                 </use>
                </svg>
                <p class="cyclops-info">
                 A rich, dark colour
                </p>
               </li>
               <li class="smell">
                <svg class="icon">
                 <use id="beer-carousel-overlay__cyclops--smell-icon" xlink:href="#svg-smell">
                 </use>
                </svg>
                <p class="cyclops-info">
                 Notes of coffee and dark chocolate
                </p>
               </li>
               <li class="taste">
                <svg class="icon">
                 <use id="beer-carousel-overlay__cyclops--taste-icon" xlink:href="#svg-lips">
                 </use>
                </svg>
                <p class="cyclops-info">
                 Smooth mouthfeel
                </p>
               </li>
              </ul>
             </div>
             <div class="beer-carousel-overlay__actions">
              <a class="button" href="https://www.fullers.co.uk/Beer/Explore-Our-Beers/Past-Masters-1926-Oatmeal-Porter">
               View
               <span class="beer-carousel-modal__beer-name">
                Past Masters 1926
               </span>
              </a>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="beer-carousel-overlay__slide">
            <div class="beer-carousel-overlay__image">
             <img src="/-/media/mainsite/Beers/Optimised/Optimised-big/Imperial-Stout.png"/>
            </div>
            <div class="beer-carousel-overlay__info">
             <h3 class="heading heading--med heading--underline-narrow-thick-alt heading--overline-narrow-alt">
              Imperial Stout
             </h3>
             <div class="beer-carousel-overlay__description">
              <p>
               A limited edition brew, Imperial Stout is a strong, dark beer with an infusion of dried rose buds for floral flavour.
              </p>
             </div>
             <div class="beer-carousel-overlay__cyclops">
              <ul>
               <li class="sight">
                <svg class="icon">
                 <use id="beer-carousel-overlay__cyclops--sight-icon" xlink:href="#svg-eye">
                 </use>
                </svg>
                <p class="cyclops-info">
                 Dark Brown / Black
                </p>
               </li>
               <li class="smell">
                <svg class="icon">
                 <use id="beer-carousel-overlay__cyclops--smell-icon" xlink:href="#svg-smell">
                 </use>
                </svg>
                <p class="cyclops-info">
                 Turkish delight, rose
                </p>
               </li>
               <li class="taste">
                <svg class="icon">
                 <use id="beer-carousel-overlay__cyclops--taste-icon" xlink:href="#svg-lips">
                 </use>
                </svg>
                <p class="cyclops-info">
                 Liquorice, caramel
                </p>
               </li>
              </ul>
             </div>
             <div class="beer-carousel-overlay__actions">
